  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0c9599f9-03a6-48a3-a467-d0ed94ac1eb3'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer10860797631073142309"><i>“You say I’ll never own you. If I win—you willingly give me that right.   <span id="freeText10860797631073142309" style="display:none"><i>“You say I’ll never own you. If I win—you willingly give me that right. You sign not only the debt agreement, but another—one that makes me your master until your last breath is taken. You do that, and I’ll give you this.”</i><br /><br />Nila Weaver’s family is indebted. Stolen, taken, and bound not by monsters but by an agreement written over six hundred years ago, she has no way out.<br /><br />She belongs to Jethro as much as she denies it.<br /><br />Jethro Hawk’s patience is running out. His inheritance gift tests, challenges, and surprises him—and not in good ways. He hasn’t leashed her but he thinks he might’ve found a way to bind her forever.<br /><br />Debts are mounting. Payment waiting.</span>

    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><u>Books in Indebted Serial should be read in order:</u><br/><b>Book 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1026427831' rel='nofollow noopener'>Debt Inheritance</a><br/>Book 2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1031223330' rel='nofollow noopener'>First Debt</a><br/>Book 3: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1108350382' rel='nofollow noopener'>Second Debt</a><br/>Book 4: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133738293' rel='nofollow noopener'>Third Debt</a><br/>Book 5: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133738309' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fourth Debt</a><br/>Book 6: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133738319' rel='nofollow noopener'>Final Debt</a><br/>Book 7: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1456095130' rel='nofollow noopener'>Indebted Epilogue</a></b><br/><br/><i><b>Debt Inheritance</b> (book 1), is the opening of a very dark modern day tale. Fashion de</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12745735001527951352" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/WintersDebtinheritance2TitlebySueBee_zps597c5d92.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419581945i/13094660.jpg" alt=" photo WintersDebtinheritance2TitlebySueBee_zps597c5d92.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/Ind2teaserxBbysb_zps28c4712a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411842798ra/11287465.gif" alt=" photo Ind2teaserxBbysb_zps28c4712a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/fd2%20story%20xB%20by%20sb_zps5g5i69yp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419581945ra/13094661.gif" alt=" photo fd2 story xB by sb_zps5g5i69yp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★ 1/2! First Debt, book 2 of 7. A dark &amp; sexual tale of Jethro’s quest to collect a centuries old debt from Nila when lust gets in the way!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“This single-minded lust between us was sacred.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books in Indebted Serial should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1026427831" rel="nofollow noopener">Debt Inheritance</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1031223330" rel="nofollow noopener">First Debt</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1108350382" rel="nofollow noopener">Second Debt</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133738293" rel="nofollow noopener">Third Debt</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133738309" rel="nofollow noopener">Fourth Debt</a><br>Book 6: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133738319" rel="nofollow noopener">Final Debt</a><br>Book 7: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1456095130" rel="nofollow noopener">Indebted Epilogue</a></b><br><br><i><b>Debt Inheritance</b> (book 1), is the opening of a very dark modern day tale. Fashion designer <b>Nila Weaver, Threads</b>, on the night of her fashion show, was introduced to a sophisticated and mysterious <b>Jethro Hawk, Jet</b> by her father and then sent off to dinner with him.<br><br>Except there was no dinner. Jethro had come to <b>to collect the debt owed to his family</b> by the Weaver family for centuries. Nila was forcefully <b>whisked from her sheltered existence to </b>his ancestor’s home, Hawksridge Hall, where she was to <b>learn more about the debt</b> and <b>how she was to repay it…</b></i><br><br><b>First Debt</b> (book 2) picks up at book 1’s ending. Nila, having been given <b>some facts</b> about the debt and coerced to <b>sexual situations</b>, is back butting head with a <b>volatile Jethro</b>. While Nila is <b>anxious to learn</b> more about her first debt repayment Jet is trying to stay <b>detached and focused.</b><br><br>There is no denying that they are <b>insanely attracted</b> to each other. Nila justifies her lust with needing a <b>way to manipulate</b> Jet while he hides behind a <b>mask of anger and hostility</b>. With glimpses into Jethro’s past and present, it’s hinted that he is on a <b>set course and cannot allow</b> himself to show any weakness towards Nila.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/fd2%20revQ%20xBQ%20by%20sb_zpsslvucqpa.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419581945ra/13094662.gif" alt=" photo fd2 revQ xBQ by sb_zpsslvucqpa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s a constant <b>power struggle</b> which Jet wins by remaining her captor, yet Nila wins by chipping away at his frozen heart. But both are <b>disposable pieces</b> in a much larger, <b>sinister game.</b> With <b>everyone watching</b> can Nila stay ahead without knowing the rules and can Jet keep aloof and in charge? And more importantly when their sexual frustrations erupt <b>how will they fight unseen forces out to destroy them?</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/di1HxBSbysb_zpsbafc04f0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408697504ra/10883662.gif" alt=" photo di1HxBSbysb_zpsbafc04f0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Jethro Hawk, Jet</b> is a product of his environment. As story unfolds we learn of an <b>abusive upbringing</b> and a different teenager conditioned to take over the family empire, any traces of <b>goodness obliterated.</b><br><br>Eight words to describe <b>Jethro: Ruthless, mercurial, complex, conflicted, determined, commanding, vengeful and tortured</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“In his late twenties, Jethro wore command like one would wear cologne.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/di1hexBSbysb_zpse2164352.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408697504ra/10883663.gif" alt=" photo di1hexBSbysb_zpse2164352.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Nila Weaver, Threads</b> fluctuates between vulnerable and naïve girl and a calculated and insightful vixen. I <b>struggled to consolidate</b> the two.<br><br>Eight words to describe <b>Nila: Naïve, focused, impressionable, frail, spirited, feisty, confused and calculated</b>.<br><br><b>First Debt</b> is their continued journey and Nila’s slow uncovering of the <b>truth and her pending demise.</b> The build-up of <b>sexual tension is intense</b> (almost setting my Kindle on fire) and ended up delivering on steam. That said, the first half of story felt <b>long-winded.</b> Story <b>ends abruptly</b> leading right to book 3, <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1108350382" rel="nofollow noopener">Second Debt</a>
</b> for the <b>continuation</b> of their story.<br><br><b>Depraved, dark</b> and <b>complex</b> Jethro! <b>Off-the-charts</b> sexual tension and situations! <b>Raw, rough</b> and <b>angry</b> sex! <b>Sinister</b> plot! <b>Spellbinding</b> story-telling! <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’ve destroyed me, Nila. And now it’s my job to make sure they don’t destroy you, too.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 4.5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 3.5 stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Plot rating: 4.5 stars<br>Dialogue rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4.5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/fd2%20revend%20xB%20by%20sb_zpsaorwsrql.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer9049506564382860302">HUGE 5 STARS!<br/>This series from Pepper Winters is just amazing, and I can't wait to read the whole series again. <br/>Reading this book again just filled my body with excitement because I know what's coming next, and even though you know what happens in it, you still can't believe what you're reading. <br/>But I love PW so much. She is my inspiration. She was the one that made me want to start writing. THANK YOU PEPPER WINTERS FOR EXISTING!! xD<br/><br/>Nila Weaver is definitely one of my favourite heroines. She's ju</span>
  <span id="freeText9049506564382860302" style="display:none">HUGE 5 STARS!<br />This series from Pepper Winters is just amazing, and I can't wait to read the whole series again. <br />Reading this book again just filled my body with excitement because I know what's coming next, and even though you know what happens in it, you still can't believe what you're reading. <br />But I love PW so much. She is my inspiration. She was the one that made me want to start writing. THANK YOU PEPPER WINTERS FOR EXISTING!! xD<br /><br />Nila Weaver is definitely one of my favourite heroines. She's just the type of character that doesn't get on my nerves because in some books you just wish the heroine would shut up and grow a pair! But Nila was refreshing, and I actually looked forward to reading from her perspective and being inside her head and knowing what she was thinking. <br />I really liked the fact that she doesn't give up either, she did run, but she hurt herself while doing in, but that just shows how much she wants her freedom and to escape from the debts paid to Jethro. <br />She has a backbone which I love from a heroine. <br /><br />Now Jethro Hawk! I mean I love alpha males, but Jethro is probably one of my favourite alpha males right now. In this book we actually get to see more of him, and being in his head just made me think 'wish things could work out for you' because it kind of made me feel like he doesn't wanna be cruel to Nila. It's like he doesn't want to make her do the debts, so that made me change my perspective of him a little bit, but to be honest I liked him in the first book although he was a little terrifying.<br /><br />Then the sex scene happened....OMG! I was waiting for it to happen.<br />I forgot all about the sex scene, and when I was reading this, I was like 'Is it gonna happen now? Is it gonna happen in this chapter?' <br />I could feel it happening!<br />What a sex scene it was! I had to have a minute to calm down because it was written really really good!<br />I can't write a good sex scene yet because I'm really inexperienced to imagine how a good sex scene is written XD But the two sex scenes DID.NOT.DISSAPOINT.AT.ALL!</span>

<div id="review_1023357138" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1023357138" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1023357138?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1023357138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12787291907373931338"><b>5 stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/c163d514-d56b-4ccc-bb4d-b22efc63cbbf_zps3f51cdae.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970136.jpg' alt=' photo c163d514-d56b-4ccc-bb4d-b22efc63cbbf_zps3f51cdae.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Pepper Winters is one of my favorite authors of the dark and twisted genre, and she didn’t disappoint when it came to <i>First Debt</i>. She took a seriously messed up book with a crazy and intense ‘hero’ (and I use that term very loosely) that was kick ass on it’s own, and wrote a second book I loved even more than the first. Jethro Hawk is not anyones hero. He’s a villain. The bad guy in the story. But maybe… just maybe he’s not quite as bad as I originally thought. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/a335f4f0-e6df-4568-b00f-8369ae51c140_zpsc18241fe.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970137.jpg' alt=' photo a335f4f0-e6df-4568-b00f-8369ae51c140_zpsc18241fe.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Nila was told to</span>
  <span id="freeText12787291907373931338" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/c163d514-d56b-4ccc-bb4d-b22efc63cbbf_zps3f51cdae.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970136.jpg" alt=" photo c163d514-d56b-4ccc-bb4d-b22efc63cbbf_zps3f51cdae.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Pepper Winters is one of my favorite authors of the dark and twisted genre, and she didn’t disappoint when it came to <i>First Debt</i>. She took a seriously messed up book with a crazy and intense ‘hero’ (and I use that term very loosely) that was kick ass on it’s own, and wrote a second book I loved even more than the first. Jethro Hawk is not anyones hero. He’s a villain. The bad guy in the story. But maybe… just maybe he’s not quite as bad as I originally thought. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/a335f4f0-e6df-4568-b00f-8369ae51c140_zpsc18241fe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970137.jpg" alt=" photo a335f4f0-e6df-4568-b00f-8369ae51c140_zpsc18241fe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nila was told to run. And she did. But it’s pretty apparent that she wasn’t going to get far. I loved that she still tried. In these circumstances, it would be easiest to roll over and heel. To play nice and try to make things as pleasant as possible. But not Nila. She is doing her best to survive and she won’t let anyone control her. Jethro holds all the cards, but she slowly gets some of the power.<br><br>As the attraction and lust between Nila and Jethro come to a head, both have to decide if thats something they can handle. They both know their fate. Neither one chose it, but they are where they are.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/1cd67c04-7133-432d-8788-8affc0110afe_zpsdfb29c92.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970138.jpg" alt=" photo 1cd67c04-7133-432d-8788-8affc0110afe_zpsdfb29c92.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>“Kiss me.”<br> “I don’t kiss my enemies.” <br>“You just fuck them?” <br>“Only if they beg.”</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br>The sexy times in <i>First Debt</i> were truly sinful. Sexy, erotic, raw, yet very sensual. When physical turns to intimacy, thats where their problems really begin. Neither one can afford any type of feelings toward one another. <br><br>Feelings. Thats what is different in this book, opposed to the first. It’s not sweet or light by any means, but the hero of the story struggles with his feelings and obligations. It didn’t seem quite as cruel as the first. I love how she made Jethro a tad bit more likable and redeemable, but still kept him on the dark side. It would be unrealistic for him to take a huge leap in such a short amount of time…. but I definitely think it’s possible in the end. I guess we’ll just have to wait and see. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/d3304cf7-295a-4a7d-a6eb-4d295b1df626_zpsa67fb0bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970139.jpg" alt=" photo d3304cf7-295a-4a7d-a6eb-4d295b1df626_zpsa67fb0bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One thing is for sure. Nila and Jethro have both changed in big ways. They’ve been impacted hugely and it’s changed the way they thing, feel and look at things. Nila is as kick ass and resilient as ever. No matter how hard things get, she never gives up. She’s a fighter until the end. I love heroines who have that backbone. Even though Nila’s gone through this terrible ordeal, she’s living. Maybe even more than she ever did in her mundane life before Jethro. <br><br>Raw. Intense. Erotic. Deliciously Dark. Forbidden at it’s finest. I love that one of the big questions from book one got revealed. It wasn’t at all what I expected, which is great. Nothing better than being shocked or surprised by the twists and turns in a book. <br><br>Once again, Pepper Winters has written a dark and enthralling story. Be prepared to read nonstop because once you start this one, you won’t be able to put it down! 5 stars for the writing, 5 stars for the characters and 5 stars for the story! I’m anxiously awaiting more Jethro and Nila! For all lovers of the twisted tales, this is one I highly recommend!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/08abc4f9-86cd-4232-87b7-03b2dc3ba333_zpsfa78f233.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416458048i/11970140.jpg" alt=" photo 08abc4f9-86cd-4232-87b7-03b2dc3ba333_zpsfa78f233.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You’ve destroyed me, Nila. And now it’s my job to make sure they don’t destroy you, too.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/910f47f1-a1e8-4ce0-8146-30b885de4588_zpsa81557bb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399861375i/9603734.jpg" alt=" photo 910f47f1-a1e8-4ce0-8146-30b885de4588_zpsa81557bb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12787291907373931338" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1031229437" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1031229437" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1031229437?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6285155-eda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1031229437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9480089402158310336"><br/><b>
  <i>** 4-4,5 "<u>x answers, 10x more questions</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re a f*cking nightmare.”<br/><br/>“Kiss me.”<br/><br/>“You’re ruining my life.”<br/><br/>“Kiss me, Jethro. Kiss me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380886323ra/3142214.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm so glad I'm one of the people that actually believed in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters' title='Pepper Winters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pepper Winters</a> and her incredible writing skills enough not to give up on this series after reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356.Debt_Inheritance__Indebted___1_' title='Debt Inheritance (Indebted, #1) by Pepper Winters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Debt Inheritance</a> and finding in it one of the most vile, nonredeemable, cruel, hardhearted male MCs <u>EVER</u>.<br/><br/>Even if you hated Book#1, even if you gave it only 1 star, I think you should g</span>
  <span id="freeText9480089402158310336" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 4-4,5 "<u>x answers, 10x more questions</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re a f*cking nightmare.”<br><br>“Kiss me.”<br><br>“You’re ruining my life.”<br><br>“Kiss me, Jethro. Kiss me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380886323ra/3142214.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm so glad I'm one of the people that actually believed in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" title="Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a> and her incredible writing skills enough not to give up on this series after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356.Debt_Inheritance__Indebted___1_" title="Debt Inheritance (Indebted, #1) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Debt Inheritance</a> and finding in it one of the most vile, nonredeemable, cruel, hardhearted male MCs <u>EVER</u>.<br><br>Even if you hated Book#1, even if you gave it only 1 star, I think you should give it another try and read this. Seriously. There are answers to some questions that will be sure to change your mind about this series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416001974ra/11875122.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Nila Weaver</u> is no longer the vertigo-ridden, obedient, gullible and naive girl that she was before she ever met the Hawks. The unspeakable things that she has been through has changed her. Being away from her glamorous life of fashion and fame has changed her. The disappointment she feels for her father now has changed her. But most importantly, <u>Jethro Hawk</u> has changed her. Immensely.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I became more than Nila Weaver. More than daughter, twin-sister, and seamstress. I became the woman who would bring down a family’s legacy. <u>I evolved into the woman who captured a Hawk.</u><br>~ NILA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><u>Jethro "Jet" Hawk</u> can feel the control he's been using as a cloak for all these years slipping away. All because of <u>Nila Weaver</u>. All because of the foreign and unwanted feeling of possession that consumes him every time she's around. All because of the lust that takes hold of his body every time she's near.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She’d given me the briefest taste of how divine it would be to own, not just her body, but her mind and soul, too. It was f*cking addicting. <u>It was f*cking twisting with my head.</u><br>~ JET</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And Nila sees right through him. She can sense the way he uses the coldness and the cruelty to cover up something warm that is deep inside him. She can sense the <i>real</i> him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I see you, Jethro Hawk. I see what you’re trying to hide, so don’t delude yourself into thinking I buy your hypocritical bullsh*t.”<br>~ NILA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The more Jet tries to push her away and out of his system, the more Nila gets under his skin, branding him, seeping through his pores into his heart. He has obligations to his family as the firstborn son. There are rules. There are debts that need extracting. And he won't be able to do what is expected of him, if this woman keeps crashing every wall he puts up between them. As mush as he tries, at the end Nila wins, and Jet is left ruined.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Nila Weaver was the sun upon my ice, turning me into a river that wanted to flow and change and grow.<br>~ JET</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The more Jet tries to push her away, the more Nila feels drawn to him. But her inner battle keeps her from ever showing the vulnerability Jet causes in her. She values her freedom way more than the inescapable feeling of lust that burns her vessels with only the single touch of this man. She is a survivor and refuses to be the pray in this game. She is the hunter. She is determined to do whatever it takes to be the hunter and take down as many Hawks as possible at the end. But does Jet really belong in that house or in that family? Does he really deserve to fall down along with the rest of the Hawk family once Nila is done?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415839018i/11854079._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The attraction, the lust, the pull is too much. <i>So they give in.</i> No longer Weaver and Hawk, no longer debtee and debtor, <i>just woman and man.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415377494i/11779921._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, they have broken the rules. They won't survive if anyone knows. Will they be able to keep it a secret? Will they be able to be...<i>partners</i>?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You’ve destroyed me, Nila. And now it’s my job to make sure they don’t destroy you, too.”<br>~ JET</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>In Book#2, both us and Nila get to know the golden-eyed <u>Kestrel "Kes" Hawk</u>, the second brother of Jet, better. He is the solar opposite of Jet. While Jet is a man with so many unresolved problems, tying him into knots and leaving him as a cold-hearted b*stard -if you will-, Kes is so warm, so nice, so polite and so understanding, he makes it very hard to believe that he is a Hawk.<br><br>While Jet tries to keep Nila away in order to hide his true self from her, Nila finds solace in Kes and he slowly becomes the only "friend" Nila has in that dreadful house.<br><br>Nila is drawn to both Kes and Jet. One is the man that she has always dreamed of, and the other is the man she would normally hate. But she likes them both. She wants them both. In different ways. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Jethro was sleek, refined —a true diamond. Kes was more of a diamond in the rough.<br>~ NILA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Nila has a plan. A plan involving either Kes or Jet to get caught in her webs and become her savior. Her rescuer.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>What better way for a Weaver to escape than for a Hawk to open her cage?<br>~ NILA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Some of you may know that I was mesmerized by Kes in Book#1. I was so much in disgust with Jet, that I was "Team Kes" when it came to Nila, so to speak.<br><br>To be honest, once we get to see the reasons behind Jet's external coldness and witness Kes' suspicious behavior throughout the book, I switched teams instantly! Now I'm "Team Jet" through and through! I have a feeling about which one of these men is honest and reliable and which one is the real snake... And I believe I'm on the right team now! ;)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Some of the big questions are answered in this book about how the Debt Inheritance all started and about the identity of Kite007. <i>(Or are they? Not so sure...)</i> But of course, this is a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" title="Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a> book, so a lot more questions are added also.<br><br>Things are getting more and more interesting with every new installment and I feel like I'm getting overly obsessed with this series! My OCD is coming back full force because of Jet and Nila, <b>DAMN THEM</b>! I want <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23489258.Second_Debt__Indebted___3_" title="Second Debt (Indebted, #3) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Second Debt</a> <b>RIGHT NOW</b>! Waiting will feel just like:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414809ra/818179.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Lastly, I'd like to talk about the reason for the 1 star subtraction from my rating:</i><br><br>You see, I am so happy that Jet is so much more lovable now. I am. I really am. But am I the only one around here that thinks his transition was rather sharp and abrupt? I wanted to experience it, I wanted to see the things about Nila that urge the change in him. <b>I couldn't do any.</b> I feel like Pepper got panicked after all the negative reviews that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356.Debt_Inheritance__Indebted___1_" title="Debt Inheritance (Indebted, #1) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Debt Inheritance</a> had gotten and tried to redeem Jethro <b>AS SOON AND AS FAST AS POSSIBLE</b>. Which didn't work for me. Thus, the minus 1 star.<br><br><b>
  <u>P.S:</u>
</b> OMG, how incredibly adorable is a jealous Jethro, right? My heart melted every damn time he was all like, <i>"Don't touch what's mine! Nila is mine, damn you!"</i> *sigh*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415285668ra/11764707.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>P.S #2:</u>
</b> Apparently <a href="http://m.youtube.com/watch?v=bR5u9jb0PJE" rel="nofollow noopener">Meg Myers ~ DESIRE</a> is the perfect song for Nila and J, according to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" title="Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a>, so I'd recommend you to listen to it while reading if you can. It certainly intensified my reading experience.<br><br>///////////////////<br><br><b>
  <u>BEFORE READING THE BOOK:</u>
</b><br><br>Totally off topic for now, but <b>I DEMAND MORE KESTREL IN THIS BOOK</b>! <br><br>You see, I secretly ship Nila and Kes. Yeah, yeah, I know. I can hear you all saying:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408645934ra/10878415.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...but I can't help it!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408645934ra/10878416.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9480089402158310336" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1028826188?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23557078-first-debt">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1028826188" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10731503293170580922"><b>5 It Just Keeps Getting Better Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416262659i/11924505._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>The only way I had a chance at surviving long enough to reap vengeance on the men who ruined my ancestors was to fight his ice with fire.<br/>I had to burn. <br/>I had to blaze.<br/>I had to cinder his beliefs and control to the ground. And smear his soul with the ashes of his sins.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416262093ra/11924395.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>If you've read the first book and found yourself unsure about where this series is going, READ THIS BOOK. First Debt just goes to further prove the genius that is the evil mind of Pepp</span>
  <span id="freeText10731503293170580922" style="display:none"><b>5 It Just Keeps Getting Better Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416262659i/11924505._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">The only way I had a chance at surviving long enough to reap vengeance on the men who ruined my ancestors was to fight his ice with fire.<br>I had to burn. <br>I had to blaze.<br>I had to cinder his beliefs and control to the ground. And smear his soul with the ashes of his sins.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416262093ra/11924395.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If you've read the first book and found yourself unsure about where this series is going, READ THIS BOOK. First Debt just goes to further prove the genius that is the evil mind of Pepper Winters. I say evil because when you get to the cliffy at the end, you'll be convinced that the woman is fucking with you. She flawlessly and seamlessly weaves a twisted and dark tale that will leave you with more questions than answers but still leave you begging for more. <b>If you haven't read the first book, DO NOT read my review as it will contain minor spoilers. I will keep it spoiler free for this book though.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416262093i/11924396._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>First Debt takes off immediately where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356.Debt_Inheritance__Indebted___1_" title="Debt Inheritance (Indebted, #1) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Debt Inheritance</a> left off. Nila Weaver is given a choice; run and if she escapes then she's released from the Debt, but if she's caught she fully gives herself over to Jethro Hawk. Mind, body, and soul.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Everything I'd been prepared for- every argument, every hardship I'd been drilled to expect- hadn't prepared me for the complication that was Nila Weaver.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Pepper Winters manages to do the seemingly impossible in this book. She gives a naive and sheltered virgin a backbone of steel and she makes you BELIEVE it. She also humanizes a cold and brutal man and gives you a peak inside his cracked armor without ruining the effect of his control.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416262093i/11924397._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">This woman had the power to ruin me. That would never be permitted. I had to ruin her first.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Both these characters are so deeply in my brain right now, I still can't stop thinking about them even a day after I finished. You really get to see both sides of the coin in their personalities. While Nila continues to develop more and more strength and truly come into her own, you also get glimpses of the vulnerable woman that has no control over her own fate. On the other hand you have a cold and ruthless Jethro, but then you get a glimpse of how he came to be the way he is and his...shall we say, motivation?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416262093i/11924398._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>While book one was more of a build and set up for the story, this one really gives you an undercurrent of romance. Don't get me wrong, since it is a Pepper Winters book after all, it's certainly not sunshine and butterflies. No. But you do have a passion that so clearly burns between two people that couldn't be more dangerous to each other.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Kiss me," I murmured...<br>"I don't kiss my enemies."<br>"You just fuck them?"<br>His mouth twitched into a roguish smile. "Only if they beg."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416286027i/11929830._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Every kiss, every touch- I was sentencing her to worse than any debt she could ever repay.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This author really knows how to build up a story that will keep you gripped to the pages from beginning to end. You'll be left with more questions with answers, but little by little you start getting more puzzle pieces...they're just not yet fitting together.<br><blockquote>
  <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">We locked eyes.<br>I shouted at her silently.<br>Cursed her wordlessly.<br><i>You feel me inside you?<br>You feel me claiming you?<br>You feel me destroying you?<br>You feel me around you?<br>You feel me undermining you?<br>You feel me making you care?</i></b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416262659ra/11924506.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>With the First Debt taking place you get to find out more about the Weaver/Hawke ancestor history that has all led to this. You get a pretty big chunk of it here, and yet there's obviously still plenty left to be answered.<br><br>You also really get that first semblance of the romance here. It may not be perfect but the foundation is being intricately laid out.<br><br>Prepare yourself for the mother of all cliffhangers too. If you thought it was bad before, you'll probably want to rip your hair out after this one. If I don't get the next book sometime soon, I'm pretty sure I'll cut a bitch LOL.<br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10731503293170580922" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1028381229" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5605450730808129658"><a href='http://amzn.to/11lngOb' rel='nofollow noopener'>Now live on Amazon!</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572488i/11813599._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was one of the readers who finished book 1 feeling shocked and a little angry with the (anti) hero Jethro Hawk. Though I never doubted that the author could redeem him in our eyes, there was <i>a lot</i> of work needed to be done before I could even forgive him, let alone like him. With this second book, the author has answered old questions, presented new ones, but most importantly, given us a reason to warm up to Jethro and both sympathize and admire Nila for her resil</span>
  <span id="freeText5605450730808129658" style="display:none"><a href="http://amzn.to/11lngOb" rel="nofollow noopener">Now live on Amazon!</a><br><br><b>4.5 stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572488i/11813599._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was one of the readers who finished book 1 feeling shocked and a little angry with the (anti) hero Jethro Hawk. Though I never doubted that the author could redeem him in our eyes, there was <i>a lot</i> of work needed to be done before I could even forgive him, let alone like him. With this second book, the author has answered old questions, presented new ones, but most importantly, given us a reason to warm up to Jethro and both sympathize and admire Nila for her resiliency. Whether or not you were a fan of the first book, I can guarantee that reading this book will present these characters in a different light…and just maybe see Jethro set on a road towards redemption. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572488i/11813600._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story begins right where the first ended: Nila is on the run and Jethro is on the hunt. They play a dangerous game of clashing wits, neither one giving an inch. Despite her time in captivity, Nila is fiercely stubborn and proud, and her resolve to get out of this hellhole never wavers while facing pain and degradation. Yes, she’s physically attracted to Jethro – and only him – but her desire for freedom is stronger and throughout the book, I really did see her struggle between revenge and freedom vs. her growing feelings for Jethro. On the other end, the author gives us an inside look into Jethro’s mindset and we’re lead to believe that he’s not so cold-hearted and cruel after all. Stuck in a crazy family that harbors a deep hatred of another household, Jethro is coerced into acting like the prodigal son and buries the <i>real</i> him deep inside. No one but Nila has the power to force him to see that who he is now isn’t who he really is and meant to be, but their thoughts can’t be voiced with the eyes of his family members carefully scrutinizing each and every one of their moves. <br><br>Except for in lust. Filthy, wicked, and sinful lust. Unlike book 1 where sex was mainly perceived to be more ritualistic than intimate, sex in here is the only place where these characters’ vulnerability can be seen. Where weakness and compromise is allowed. Both Nila and Jethro are equals in lust.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572488i/11813601._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But that creates a big problem: just how do they deal with their feelings for each other when they’re both smacked with problems: Jethro and his family, Nila and her freedom? This is where I think the author’s brilliant writing comes in, evoking tormenting and agonizing feelings because of the dichotomy presented. I really felt for both of these characters – especially Jethro – and their terrible situation. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572488i/11813602._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Old questions like the reason behind the debt inheritance, Kite’s identity, etc... will all be answered but at the same time these answers lead to even more mystery that had me questioning what I knew already. When you read this book, please keep in mind that this is a series that’s dark first, romance second. It’s because of how twisty and messed up this entire situation is that makes any possible romance THAT much more precious. <br><br><u>First Debt</u> is the 2nd installment in the Indebted serial and not a standalone. You must read <u>Debt Inheritance</u> first. The author has prefaced in all of these books that cliffhangers are to be expected and while it’ll leave you desperate for the next one, it’ll also be a satisfying reading experience as each of these books has a full beginning, middle, and end. <br><br><i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_1024679421" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1024679421" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1024679421?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-erotica">dark-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=mind-f-ckery">mind-f-ckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=gamma-hero">gamma-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1024679421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8026449537604200029"><b>5 Indebted Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415629997i/11821530._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo FIRSTDEBTQUOTEY_zps02164e3a.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Wow – what a ride! After the shock and awe of the first book, Debt Inheritance, the second book in this darkly mysterious series really gets the story flowing. In book one we were very much under starter’s orders with plenty of world building and the scene being set – now in Second Debt we’re rapidly galloping down the straight with plenty of hurdles to leap along the way.<br/><br/><blockquote>He stepped from the sun’s glare, his teeth sparkling like diamonds. “Now…run.” <br/><br/>… <br/><br/>… <br/><br/>I ran.</blockquote><br/><br/>This is how we ended</span>
  <span id="freeText8026449537604200029" style="display:none"><b>5 Indebted Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415629997i/11821530._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo FIRSTDEBTQUOTEY_zps02164e3a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Wow – what a ride! After the shock and awe of the first book, Debt Inheritance, the second book in this darkly mysterious series really gets the story flowing. In book one we were very much under starter’s orders with plenty of world building and the scene being set – now in Second Debt we’re rapidly galloping down the straight with plenty of hurdles to leap along the way.<br><br><blockquote>He stepped from the sun’s glare, his teeth sparkling like diamonds. “Now…run.” <br><br>… <br><br>… <br><br>I ran.</blockquote><br><br>This is how we ended the first book and how we begin the second – with Nila running for her life, her freedom and her sanity and Jethro chasing her down like the prey that she is. She’s not going to give up without a fight and is constantly battling to get one over on Jethro and often succeeds but she never really stood a chance and soon finds herself back in his clutches once more, albeit after gaining a minor victory of her own. <br><br>This is such a devilishly enigmatic series which is constantly playing with my mind and, no doubt, Nila’s. After her nightmarish introduction to the Brotherhood and all the degradation that it entailed, they now treat her like an honoured guest and are charming and friendly all the time knowing she has numerous ‘debts’ to repay and will ultimately pay with her head. It’s a curious juxtaposition between courteous gentlemen and deadly captors. No wonder the poor girl is more than a little lost and confused. <br><br>You’ve got to hand it to Nila – she’s definitely one of life’s copers. I think it’s safe to say that the poor girl was terrified and overwhelmed in Debt Inheritance but she definitely comes into her own in Second Debt. She’s not prepared to go down without a fight and she’s determined to take as many Hawks down with her as she possibly can. After her cossetted and stifling upbringing with her family, her current situation, however deadly it is, does offer some semblance of freedom and contentment, all barring the death sentence of course! She’s able to roam the mansion at will and can relax and do what she pleases. She constantly wars with Jethro for the upper hand and finds some chinks in his icy armour that she’s able to exploit. <br><br>Jethro was very much the fiercely stoic and demonic captor in Debt Inheritance with absolutely no redeeming features at all other than his handsome face and fit body. He’s the thief of Nila’s freedom, the instigator of her ultimate destruction but in Second Debt we get a far deeper insight to this man and find that not everything is as it first seems. He is as much a pawn in this deadly plan set in motion centuries before as Nila is – he’s still willing to carry out her sentence but we get to learn far more about how conflicted he is about all this. Not least about his overwhelming sexual attraction to her and the unexpected and fierce possessiveness he feels towards her. <br><br>This was such an incredibly compelling read that I absolutely devoured this in the space of 24 hours, such was my inability to put this down. I constantly found myself putting myself in Nila’s place and that’s not something many books inspire me to do anymore. Nila’s and Jethro’s connection is positively incendiary, like fire and ice, and neither of them has experienced anything like this before as the mysterious story peels back a few layers while still keeping plenty secret for the books to come. Nila has paid off the first brutal debt leaving her bleeding and in pain and this is supposed to be the most lenient punishment she has to endure – I fear for her when it comes to paying the second debt. <br><br>So much happens in this book – we get to know Jethro’s brothers much better, the mysterious Kite007 is finally unveiled and more is revealed about the Weaver’s apparent atrocities of the past. I find this so fascinating – how can this ‘debt’ transcend the centuries and the laws of the land and how can all parties be so willing to let it stand? I feel there is more to be revealed yet. This really does have the mysterious oppressive feeling of a gothic horror novel – set in an isolated sprawling mansion in the British countryside with the requisite stuffed kills adorning the walls and the dark ominous presence of Jethro, her lover and ultimately her executioner. What a truly original and thrilling series this is turning out to be. Steeped in mystery, eroticism and and intrigue, this really is Pepper Winters, Queen of the Darkness, at her finest. Absolutely can’t wait for Second Debt as this highly addictive story edges closer to it’s final destination. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415643213i/11823271._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo firstdebtpepper_zpsbf1ecd26.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415732205i/11837223._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo firstddebt5stars_zpsc12a6c07.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8026449537604200029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1039086167" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1039086167" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1039086167?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1039086167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer217285741903178713"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416139854i/11900642.jpg' width='400' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This was the ultimate test. The Debt Inheritance was more than history and payments — it was an important sequence of events that every firstborn Hawk had to complete in order to inherit his legacy.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416139854i/11900643.png' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>“First Debt”</i> is the second installment in the <i>“Indebted”</i> series by Pepper Winters. <br/><br/>Even if I still think the premise is partially plausible, I enjoyed this book, even more than the first one. Plausible or not, it's an interesting and unique premise.<br/> <br/><i>“First Debt”</i> is not as sick d</span>
  <span id="freeText217285741903178713" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416139854i/11900642.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This was the ultimate test. The Debt Inheritance was more than history and payments — it was an important sequence of events that every firstborn Hawk had to complete in order to inherit his legacy.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416139854i/11900643.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“First Debt”</i> is the second installment in the <i>“Indebted”</i> series by Pepper Winters. <br><br>Even if I still think the premise is partially plausible, I enjoyed this book, even more than the first one. Plausible or not, it's an interesting and unique premise.<br> <br><i>“First Debt”</i> is not as sick disturbing like the first book. It’s more intense and it’s more between Jethro and Nila. The story picks up right where the first book ends. <br><br>Nila is on the run. She runs for her life and for her freedom. Jethro hunts her, obviously wanting to catch his prey. He is eager to teach her a lesson. Both of them know who will win, but for Nila this game is not about winning, it’s about fight and survival. If the first book presented a terrified Nila, here Nila is determined to fight at all costs for what she wants, for what it’s right.<br><br>Jethro realize how much Nila wants her freedom and he knows she's ready to do anything for it. He is surprised by her actions. She intrigues him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I had to burn. I had to blaze. I had to cinder his beliefs and control to the ground. And smear his soul with the ashes of his sins.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Nila wants not only to win, she also wants vengeance. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416140537i/11900765._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's not the only one who wants to run. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Unlike my prey, I faced my demons and embraced them. I made them work for me, rather than control me, and forced them to submit by bowing at my fucking feet.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jethro was all his life his father's son. He knows his obligations as the firstborn son. He is the debtor and Nila is the debtee and he also knows she can’t be more...<br><br>Nila is the only one who brings to surface another face of Jethro. <br>If in the first book, Jethro seemed unredeemable, the author makes him more human in this book. We get to see a new Jethro, the real Jethro. <br><br>Both Nila and Jethro are struggling with their feelings. Nila wants to be free, but her feelings for her captor are growing every day. Jethro doesn’t know who he is anymore, especially since his captive continues to steal his power. Nila makes him question everything – who he is and what he feels. She sees him, the real Jethro and what he’s trying to hide. Jethro realizes how much Nila change him, but no one can ever know that if he wants to protect what they got. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416140537i/11900766.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She owned me. Her laughable rage, her stupid sense of fairness. Somehow, she’d ensorcelled me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>None of them can’t deny their chemistry. When they are together intimately, everything disappears. When they are together, each one of them can be real.<br> <br>Jethro wants to keep Nila, to protect her, but in order to do that he must keep her at arm’s length. They have to learn to deal with their feelings in order to survive. Both of them!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416140537i/11900767.png" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I must say I really liked the new Jethro. Jethro’s character is so well developed in this second book. If you dislike or even hate him in the first book, here, you will empathize with him. I really did! You will get to know him better, understand him and also understand his choices. Like I said before, he is more human in this installment. He is compassionate and even caring with Nila. I absolutely loved how possessive and jealous he is at some point. Needless to say, I really liked him in this book. <br><br>Nila is a great heroine. She is strong, even if she obviously has her fears. She is ready to fight and even do anything to be free. But she also is attracted to her enemy and this attraction can be dangerous. I truly felt for her. I liked her and I liked her a lot!<br><br>Both Jethro and Nila felt real to me and their relationship felt more intense than ever in this installment. <br><br>You will get some answers and you will find out what exactly means this “first debt”, but like me, I’m pretty sure in the end you will have other questions. <br><br>This series is really good, addictive and I can’t wait for the next installment.<br><br>Overall, a fantastic read!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We were both chained to a future we didn’t want, and there was no way out—for either of us.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="217285741903178713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=freakin-cliffies">freakin-cliffies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-trust-feifei">i-trust-feifei</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=mystery-suspense">mystery-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=im-gonna-need-therapy">im-gonna-need-therapy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=mind-fuck">mind-fuck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=motha-whiplash-emotions">motha-whiplash-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-recs">buddy-recs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1031323794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6015778153672215687"><b>4.5 HAWK STARS! ★★★★☆</b><br/><br/>♥ Buddy Read with my awesome bestie <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1105919283?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Penelope</a>! ♥<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416039531i/11881165.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"This wasn't about the chase. We all knew who would win. It was about defiance."</b>
</i><br/><br/>After being let down by my previous highly anticipated read, naturally I was wary about picking up another sequel by one of my favorite authors. And thank heavens Pepper Winters did not disappoint at all. After Book 1 that left many readers in shock with Jethro's downright stone-cold demeanour, this one definitely shine a whole new light on him a</span>
  <span id="freeText6015778153672215687" style="display:none"><b>4.5 HAWK STARS! ★★★★☆</b><br><br>♥ Buddy Read with my awesome bestie <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1105919283?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Penelope</a>! ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416039531i/11881165.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"This wasn't about the chase. We all knew who would win. It was about defiance."</b>
</i><br><br>After being let down by my previous highly anticipated read, naturally I was wary about picking up another sequel by one of my favorite authors. And thank heavens Pepper Winters did not disappoint at all. After Book 1 that left many readers in shock with Jethro's downright stone-cold demeanour, this one definitely shine a whole new light on him and will have you begging for more Jethro by the end of it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>First Debt</b>
</i> picks up right after the end of Book 1 where we have Nila running for her freedom as Jethro begins his hunt for her. In an almost dramatic manner where Jethro hunts her down on his horse, an attempt to escape proves to be a futile one on Nila's part (and not to mention some Hunger Games imagery when Nila starts climbing a tree LOL). These two certainly had each other at their throats as neither one would back down and further fueled with lust, there was no denying their attraction for each other.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416043073ra/11881884.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jethro's character definitely took a turn in this book</b> as we got to tap deeper into his psyche and getting glimpses behind those cold walls. Although I was a little thrown off with the change in Jethro almost taking effect from the first chapter itself, what I appreciated was the author still <b>allowed us to see the struggles Jethro constantly faced with his actions towards Nila.</b> That for me, felt realistic as I didn't feel that the author drastically changed Jethro just because he was such a cold-hearted bastard in the first book. Which by the way, he's still pretty much one in this one and that pleases me. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"There was no way any other man could ever compete with the elegant chillness of Jethro. He was exactly like the iceberg he favoured, only in different lights, more truth shone. Some bright and light and binding, others black and deep and terrifying."</i>
</blockquote><br>The only person who could possibly be close enough to burn those cold walls down is Nila who constantly challenges him and pushes him to the brink of allowing his <i>real</i> self to surface. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I see you, Jethro Hawk. I see what you're trying to hide, so don't delude yourself into thinking I buy your hypocritical bullshit."</i>
</blockquote><br>What I felt was truly compelling about this read was the <b>power play between Jethro and Nila</b>. What started out as Jethro seizing full control over Nila, the author certainly had the tables turning in this instalment. You'll be wondering who's the hunter and prey now as Nila plays a dangerous game, knowing where to push Jethro's buttons. Neither one is willing to relinquish control and that really brought out an <b>explosive dynamic</b> between these two that is equally agonizing and sizzling to watch.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"We're on even ground. Orgasm for an orgasm. Don't think it gives you power, because it doesn't."</i>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391215108ra/8351972.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, the constant appearance of <b>Kestrel</b> who's the polar opposite of Jethro didn't really do much for me because I've always been on #teamjethro (I'm all for the bad guys, good guys kinda bore me LOL). But I'm all for it if it's gonna fan some fire of jealousy in that ice-cold Jethro. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With this one shedding light on some unanswered questions from the prior book and presenting new ones, <b>this book surely gripped me from the get-go and I simply couldn't put it down.</b> Ms. Pepper continues to dish out her brilliant yet twisted writing that leaves me <i>begging</i> for more. <br><br>And as for the reveal of Kite's identity, this one definitely proves to be a game-changer move and I absolutely cannot wait to see where the series will take us now. <br><br><i>First Debt is part of the Indebted series and cannot be read as a standalone.</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="6015778153672215687" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107153076?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23557078-first-debt">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Dark, Suspenseful Romances</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dom-sub-bdsm">dom-sub-bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dark-romance-nov-2014-challenge">dark-romance-nov-2014-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107153076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9764845248099589415">Picking up where the first book left off, 'First Debt' continues in the same addicting, suspenseful manner that is Ms. Winters' hallmark. I was so engrossed in this second installment of the series that I kept reading straight through until the early morning hours, when I finally lost the battle to sheer exhaustion and fell asleep with my iPad on my chest and glasses still on. When I woke up after a few hours of sleep, I picked up where I left off, not willing to leave my bed or brush my teeth u</span>
  <span id="freeText9764845248099589415" style="display:none">Picking up where the first book left off, 'First Debt' continues in the same addicting, suspenseful manner that is Ms. Winters' hallmark. I was so engrossed in this second installment of the series that I kept reading straight through until the early morning hours, when I finally lost the battle to sheer exhaustion and fell asleep with my iPad on my chest and glasses still on. When I woke up after a few hours of sleep, I picked up where I left off, not willing to leave my bed or brush my teeth until I had finished this book. It's that great!<br /><br />I was captivated, watching Nila's transformation in this book from a damsel in distress to a force to be reckoned with. She is not the timid wallflower waiting to be rescued that we met in the first book. This kitten has grown some claws and is giving Jethro as good as she gets. I'm loving this ferocious, strong, and resilient side of Nila. <br /><br />Jethro also seems to be transforming before our eyes. He's still cold and at times cruel, but this installment reveals a more human side to him. Like in the first book, you'll still hate him at times, but now you'll love him too. Nila has really cracked his steely exterior, allowing glimpses of Jethro's inner turmoil. <br /><br />Where the first installment left me feeling sexually frustrated, in book 2 Ms. Winters delivers for readers in a big way! Finally giving in to their desire, Nila and Jethro go at it like bunnies on crack! They have some of the best angry-sex I've ever read. Two words: PANTY MELTING!<br /><br />A few big revelations, like Kite's true identity, the first debt "payment" and Nila's developing friendship with Kes, drew me even deeper into this twisted story of revenge. Oh, and the steamy sex! Did I mention that already?<br /><br />I have to admit, I have a hard time envisioning bad-ass English bikers that live in a mansion and dress and act like aristocrats. Biker gangs and polo matches don't mix in my mind. That is hard for me to reconcile in my little head. It doesn't detract from the story in my opinion, just makes me smile. Hell, if Ms. Winters wrote about men wearing pink Easter Bunny costumes and picking wild flowers, they'd probably be real bad-asses! That's talent!<br /><br />So, I'll be anxiously awaiting the next installment. I can't wait to see where this story is going next! I'm completely hooked!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9764845248099589415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
