              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1089029280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17553728899505366632"><b>5 bat-shit crazy STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420760762i/13258902.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’d been taught to be the master of my emotions. I prided myself on embracing all that he taught me. One little Weaver bitch would not undermine me. This was the way of our world.<br/>My world.<br/>Her world.<br/>No matter how she bewitched me, no matter how she turned my body and willpower against me, I wouldn’t give in.<br/>She’d learn that soon enough.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Yeah. Good luck with that one stud. You're a glutton for punishment if you actually think Ms. Winters doesn't have other plans </span>
  <span id="freeText17553728899505366632" style="display:none"><b>5 bat-shit crazy STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420760762i/13258902.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’d been taught to be the master of my emotions. I prided myself on embracing all that he taught me. One little Weaver bitch would not undermine me. This was the way of our world.<br>My world.<br>Her world.<br>No matter how she bewitched me, no matter how she turned my body and willpower against me, I wouldn’t give in.<br>She’d learn that soon enough.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Yeah. Good luck with that one stud. You're a glutton for punishment if you actually think Ms. Winters doesn't have other plans for you. Just hold on tight and pray for mercy...that's what we do every time we open one of her books. Just sayin'.<br><br>A new <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/124092-indebted" rel="nofollow noopener">Indebted</a> book and I'm chronically late reading it. I have no clue why, because I love her unusual anti-heroes like nothing else and yet I need ages to pick them up. Here is another New Year's resolution...read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7151973.Pepper_Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Pepper Winters</a> books as soon as they drop! :D<br><br>Ok, let's do this.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420895792i/13287623.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We start right where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356-debt-inheritance" rel="nofollow noopener">Debt Inheritance</a> left off. <br><br>Nila is on the run! With Jethro is in hot pursuit. <br><br>Of course with a little help from half a docent foxhounds and a horse. No one said this was going to be a fair chase after all. But Nila continues to be a surprise for him. She is strong willed and tougher than he would have ever imagined. It’s not without trouble that he finds her and the real problems are only just starting to emerge.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This wasn't about the chase. We all knew who would win. It was about defiance. The word that I never knew or put into practice until last night, but now I lived and breathed it. I would be the most defiant thorn, stabbing holes in Jethro's carefully made plans.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It follows a ruthless mind-game and basically a battle of wills. The good stuff.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He claimed he was cold-hearted and impervious. He lied.<br>I'll show him. I'll prove he's as ill-equipped to play this charade as I am.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Jethro, oh dear Jethro!</b><br><br>That boy is in so much trouble and it is beautiful to see it all unravel. I have to say his little Jekyll and Hyde thing he has going in his head is amusing to say the least. <br><br>One second he is the cold hearted arsehole we love to hate and the next he shows almost human like tendencies. What gives? Not complaining, mind you. But the cracks he is showing might be a bit premature. I would have loved a smoother transition, to be honest. But I did love seeing his role in the family, his troubles and reasons. That made it all more plausible and easier to stomach, I guess.<br><br>But all in all a really interesting character and that first debt he collected? I don't know, but if that was the easy one? Oh boy!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420894611i/13287274.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Nila bad-ass Weaver</b><br><br>Where did you hide those balls all these years? I'm so glad you finally use them. Rock on girlfriend!<br><br>Nila grows stronger and more focused by the minute and that's saying something. Most people would crack under these circumstances, but for some reason this woman is a fast learner and can adjust like nothing I've seen before.<br><br>But despite all that is happening I have a feeling like they evened out the playing field and it just makes playing games so much more entertaining, doesn’t it?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We would keep on ruining each other.<br>We would keep on desecrating debts and vows.<br>And we would keep on fucking up our future until nothing but horror remained.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What else can I say about this book? First and foremost, I loved a lot more than the last one. Especially Nila seems a lot more grounded and less all over the place. We get to see who she is, who she becomes and I love to see the fight in her.<br><br>Jethro on the other hand has this rather <i>fast</i> change of heart. The pure evil we loved to hate in the first instalment seems to have taken flight...puff and gone...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420911149i/13289916.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But regardless this book kept my pulse up and not necessarily because bad shit happened, but because I was afraid of what might happen. There is this constant undercurrent of danger lurking and it's rather amazing to see such skill in an author, but on the other hand I was scared as hell. Oh my poor nerves...<br><br><i>First Debt</i> is not a book for casual reading or even skimming through. Every other sentence could be quoted. Seriously, you don't even want to see all the passages I highlighted. And I felt like paying extra attention because I was afraid of missing something important.<br><br>Also, the ending...HOLY SHIT! I screamed like a little girl and I'm still a little giddy. I love this shit! And yes, I swear a lot. Sorry, not sorry. ;P<br><br><br><i>**Off topic: one of my New Year's resolutions is working...I'm taking notes. Can you tell? ;D</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1213766758" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1213766758" />
    <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog"><img alt="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420222674p2/38657470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1213766758?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23557078-first-debt">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=another-damn-cliffy">another-damn-cliffy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=must-just-be-me">must-just-be-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=audio-books">audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=1-and-a-half-stars">1-and-a-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1213766758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9381492909136021972"><b>1.5 stars, but should I be generous and give it 2?</b><br/><br/>I know, I know. I gave a rather scathing review of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356.Debt_Inheritance__Indebted___1_' title='Debt Inheritance (Indebted, #1) by Pepper Winters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Debt Inheritance</a>, so why on Earth did I read <i>First Debt</i>? Apparently I’m a glutton for punishment because I decided to give this book a chance when I saw it was available at the library. I figured I had nothing to lose except maybe some of my precious reading time, because…free. Oh, and it was the audio book version so…bonus! <br/><br/>Anyway, I was hoping this book would surprise me, and I admit I was a li</span>
  <span id="freeText9381492909136021972" style="display:none"><b>1.5 stars, but should I be generous and give it 2?</b><br><br>I know, I know. I gave a rather scathing review of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21400356.Debt_Inheritance__Indebted___1_" title="Debt Inheritance (Indebted, #1) by Pepper Winters" rel="nofollow noopener">Debt Inheritance</a>, so why on Earth did I read <i>First Debt</i>? Apparently I’m a glutton for punishment because I decided to give this book a chance when I saw it was available at the library. I figured I had nothing to lose except maybe some of my precious reading time, because…free. Oh, and it was the audio book version so…bonus! <br><br>Anyway, I was hoping this book would surprise me, and I admit I was a little curious to see how and when Nila grows a backbone. I may have liked this book a little more than the first, but basically <i>First Debt</i> did little to change my opinion of this series. <br><br>Nila proves she’s strong all right, but she’s still gullible, wishy washy, and really quite dim. She completely depleted my stores of patience and understanding. <br><br>We get to see more glimpses into Jethro’s thoughts, which is nice, but it’s not enough to redeem him. Despite his despicable, abusive, and often just weird behavior, I think we’re supposed to feel sorry for him for developing feelings for his captive. Like I couldn’t see that coming from a mile away as noted in my previous review. And the big plot twisting cliffhanger? Yeah, I totally predicted that while reading the first book also. There are remaining puzzles that might appeal to other readers though.<br><br>Obviously, I didn’t care for the story, but the writing style put me off as well. It’s writing like this that had me rolling my eyes and groaning out loud (and not in a good way).<blockquote>
  <b>“Fuck me, please. I’m begging. I need it. I need you. I’ve never needed anything as much as you filling me. Jethro, I’ll die if you don’t fuck me this very minute.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I’m also wondering. Is this what’s considered purple prose?<b>
  <blockquote>I sank inside with a barbarous impale. She screamed. I groaned. We both collapsed into one another. Falling, falling, swirling, swirling, we took each other prisoner. Punishing our bodies, focusing on one blistering goal.</blockquote>
</b><br>And then there’s the obligatory your-penis-is-way-too-big for me dialog, only with a decidedly unsexy, harsh selfishness thrown in. <blockquote>
  <b>“Oh, God. No. Stop,” she cried. Her hips tried to dislodge my size.<br><br>“I can’t stop.”<br><br>“It hurts.” Her breath was cool against my fevered flesh.<br><br>“Let me in!” I thrust again, gritting my teeth.</b>
</blockquote><br>And on that note, I’m officially done with this series.<br><br><a href="http://readingfrenzyblog.com" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458784026i/18530130.jpg" alt="Reading Frenzy Book Blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9381492909136021972" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=jackass-heroes">jackass-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=super-steamy">super-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=hells-yeah-alphas">hells-yeah-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=love-hate-relationship">love-hate-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=heart-breaking">heart-breaking</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1188532104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10997632691049558642"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399754i/773926._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.25 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423086572i/13586296._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>'This woman had the power to ruin me. That would never be permitted. I had to ruin her first.'<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410228282i/11077080._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series!! It has me completely hooked. If you have read the previous book, you know it ends with a cliffhanger. Nila has the chance to escape if she can run to edge of the property before she is caught. If she doesn't make it, Jethro will own her completely and Nila mustn't c</span>
  <span id="freeText10997632691049558642" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399754i/773926._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.25 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423086572i/13586296._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>'This woman had the power to ruin me. That would never be permitted. I had to ruin her first.'<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410228282i/11077080._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series!! It has me completely hooked. If you have read the previous book, you know it ends with a cliffhanger. Nila has the chance to escape if she can run to edge of the property before she is caught. If she doesn't make it, Jethro will own her completely and Nila mustn't complain. To the surprise of Jethro, she actually runs. He is intrigued by her determination and her fight. No matter what, she doesn't give up her hope for freedom. Nila is figuring out how she wants to play this game. She is tired of losing to Jethro. She wants to survive and make it to the end. Her strategy is now to make Jethro fall for her in order to be able to control him. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Today is your First Debt, Ms. Weaver. The Debt Inheritance has begun."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I can't tell you how much more I enjoyed this book than the previous one. It was just so good. I absolutely loved getting more into Jethro's mind and finally being able to understand him. He's changed quite a bit since the first book and it was in a believable way. I didn't think I would be able to like him at all, but I am definitely warming up to him. Things are getting a whole lot more interesting. Despite this book being so twisted, I was surprised by how much I was enjoying the sexual tension between Nila and Jethro. It was really hot and was very well done. I also really liked Nila. I love seeing her grow more stronger and more sure of herself. There was one scene that really made me feel for her. I don't know in what state I'd be in if I were in her shoes, so I really admire her resilience. Together these two were intense and I was really happy with how well I was able to connect with them both.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423088171ra/13586465.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“We would keep on ruining each other.<br>We would keep on desecrating debts and vows.<br>And we would keep on fucking up our future until nothing but horror remained.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>In order to protect each other, they want to keep things purely physical, but their feelings are evolving, and that can be very dangerous for the both of them. I don't know what will happen next, but I am extremely excited to continue this series. I am very much liking the direction of the story. I liked the growth of both the characters, and the start of something romantic between Nila dnd Jethro. There were definitely some dark and horrifying things that took place in this book, so this isn't for everyone. I was glad that some of the questions I had were answered, but holy hell, do I have a ton more of them now. That ending...I had my guesses but I didn't see that coming. I can't wait to dig into the next book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410228282i/11077080._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>***WARNING: Contains scenes with violence.***<br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10997632691049558642" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1096120256" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1096120256" />
    <a title="The Hopeless Romantics Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16884018-the-hopeless-romantics-book-blog"><img alt="The Hopeless Romantics Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367177114p2/16884018.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1096120256?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The Hopeless Romantics Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="The Hopeless Romantics Book Blog" href="/user/show/16884018-the-hopeless-romantics-book-blog">The Hopeless Romantics Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16884018-the-hopeless-romantics-book-blog?shelf=arc-received-for-honest-review">arc-received-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16884018-the-hopeless-romantics-book-blog?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16884018-the-hopeless-romantics-book-blog?shelf=5-hearts">5-hearts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16884018-the-hopeless-romantics-book-blog?shelf=november-14">november-14</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1096120256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12010834370897280250"><b>Review: Surj Harvey</b><br/><br/>Facebook: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessRomanticsBookBlog'>https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessR...</a><br/>Blog: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessRomanticsBookBlog'>https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessR...</a><br/><br/>Where the hell do I start with this review? With the plot? With him? With her? With them? With Pepper's fantastic writing? Honestly, my head is spinning, my emotions are all over the place. This book has quite literally left me gob smacked, speechless, dumb founded... what in God's name do I do now? I feel lost... quite literally lost and I cannot believe this author chose to end th</span>
  <span id="freeText12010834370897280250" style="display:none"><b>Review: Surj Harvey</b><br /><br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessRomanticsBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessR...</a><br />Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessRomanticsBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/TheHopelessR...</a><br /><br />Where the hell do I start with this review? With the plot? With him? With her? With them? With Pepper's fantastic writing? Honestly, my head is spinning, my emotions are all over the place. This book has quite literally left me gob smacked, speechless, dumb founded... what in God's name do I do now? I feel lost... quite literally lost and I cannot believe this author chose to end the book there!!!! I mean there... how could you???? With all the revelations that have come to light, all I keep thinking about is all the avenues the story line could take and trust me, there are quite a few. Unfortunately, whichever way our characters go, one thing is for certain: Debts will have to be repaid. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"A pet can only hate for so long. But ply it with warmth, safety, kindness and good food and soon..you'll have no choice but to let go of that hate in your heart and embrace the life we're giving you." <br /></i>
  </b>
</blockquote> So who remembers how the first book in the series finished? Yup, that word... RUN!!! I couldn't wait to see the fallout of this challenge but my heart already knew who the winner would be: Jethro... the man who scared the ever loving life out of me. Looking back at my review for "Debt Inheritance," I remember saying how much I loathed and feared him. How he was a monster, a wolf in sheep's clothing. I don't recall saying anything positive about him at all. So what the hell happened? 15%... 15% into "First Debt" was all it took and I'd softened towards him... yup, warped mind and all . I mean really? WTF? Had I so quickly forgotten what this man had done, what he was capable of doing and what he had every intention of delivering? No I hadn't but he managed to wrap me around his little finger pretty quickly and that was it... I was gone!!! Lost to him and nothing he said or did would sway me otherwise. I was done for. <br /><br />Nila's character grew a lot in this book and she really came into her own. The strength and defiance she displayed was just awe inspiring. Nila was smart, brave and feisty and she would not accept her fate, fighting this stupidity every step of the way... taking any path necessary to gain her freedom. But what would happen when 'need' got in the way? Would her resolver falter? Would she crumble in front of the enemy? I was praying not for her sake. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This was a battle. Every time we touched, licked and eventually fucked, it would be war. And only one victor would come out alive. I had every intention of winning. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />"First Debt" was about a fight for power. It was a war between right and wrong, a battle with the past, an internal struggle with emotions. I was giddy with excitement as victories were gained. But there were times my heart bottomed out as the characters continued to play with fire, dancing so very close to the flame. But with any battle, there could only be one winner and unfortunately, in this case (ducks head as missiles head my way) I was on Jethro's side!!! I know, I know ...crazy huh!!! But you'll get it once you read the book... I promise. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I should have known it was the beginning of the end. I should have guessed how badly she would ruin me. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />This second book really mixed things up for me, showing sides to characters that shocked me, taking the story line in directions that surprised me and as a bonus, I got answers to so many questions that had driven me bat shit crazy in "Debt Inheritance." Who was Kite? What was the deal with Kestrel? Where did the debts originate from and what did the repayment entail? Yes all will be revealed in this installment. Slowly but surely, everything started to slot into place and finally, I was getting it.<br /><br />Before I finish up my review, I have to mention one particular scene... I can't go into detail but OMG... the power behind it, the words, the intensity, the raw emotion coursing through those few pages... my heart thumped in my head, I couldn't look away... it was almost as if I was entranced by what I was reading... it was perfection ... just perfection and I really hope it has the same effect on you as it did me... trust me, you'll know when you get to it. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Kiss me."<br />"I don't kiss my enemies."<br />"You just fuck them?"<br />Only if they beg."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Pepper Winters has yet again excelled in her writing abilities and has quite literally delivered to her readers a literary masterpiece. I can't imagine anyone not being happy with this next installment. It was dark, twisted, f**ked up and 100% addictive and I couldn't rate it anything less than ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12010834370897280250" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1106796552" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1106796552" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1106796552?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1106796552" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16247743689394780525"><br/><b>4.25 Indebted Stars!</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/BCF74F12-083E-46EB-AE69-A03D722DC674_zpsxxcpswhz.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416183035i/11908395._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo BCF74F12-083E-46EB-AE69-A03D722DC674_zpsxxcpswhz.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Well, I'm happy to say I like Jethro much better in this book. I was a bit apprehensive going into it as he wasn't an anti-hero I particularly liked (and yes, I like many anti-heroes). <br/><br/><br/><br/>The following contains spoilers for the ending of book one-<br/><br/><br/>This book picks up right where the last left off. Nila is within the clutches of the Hawk family, Jethro specifically being her captor. She continues to fight for her way out of this nightmare. After a confrontation on the property,</span>
  <span id="freeText16247743689394780525" style="display:none"><br><b>4.25 Indebted Stars!</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/BCF74F12-083E-46EB-AE69-A03D722DC674_zpsxxcpswhz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416183035i/11908395._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BCF74F12-083E-46EB-AE69-A03D722DC674_zpsxxcpswhz.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Well, I'm happy to say I like Jethro much better in this book. I was a bit apprehensive going into it as he wasn't an anti-hero I particularly liked (and yes, I like many anti-heroes). <br><br><br><br>The following contains spoilers for the ending of book one-<br><br><br>This book picks up right where the last left off. Nila is within the clutches of the Hawk family, Jethro specifically being her captor. She continues to fight for her way out of this nightmare. After a confrontation on the property, Jethro has given Nila a chance to escape and she's taken it. Forty-five minutes...time for the hunt....<br><br><br>We get a lot more character development with Jethro in this book and I think I really needed it. Gradually we are trickle fed Jet's inner conflicts between upholding his family tradition of making the Weavers pay, of pleasing his god-awful father, and battling between the coldness within and the all-consuming heat that Nila causes within his soul. We still don't know deep down what was done to "train" Jethro to be ruthless...to instill the coldness within for the first-born son to be able to extract each and every debt from the Weaver captive. <br><br><br>Can Jethro continue to maintain the physical and emotional boundaries, play by the rules, extract each and every debt? Can Nila hold strong to her inner self, not allowing Jethro to own her mind? He can have her body but not her soul... But will her mind too betray her? Can she resist his pull? It's an endless fight for control. Each of them want to win the upper hand but the physical pull between them may be both of their demise. Who will win in the end? Will neither?<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=6CC243F0-3904-402A-A829-911A7407460C_zpspfugxoa3.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392488120ra/8568343.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This book is fairly dark, I'd go "medium rare" on the darkness factor. We finally get some erotic moments that I've been painfully holding out for. Ms Winters is the master of painting an intensely erotic, all-consuming sexual scene. This series promises to give the readers a lot of twists and turns, but I guess with it being a six book series, we've got lots of time and won't see a resolution anytime soon. I just hope my book attention deficit disorder can hold strong that long...<br><br><br>Looking forward to <b>Indebted #3, Second Debt,</b> to be released early 2015. <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16247743689394780525" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1034800738" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1034800738" />
    <a title="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner"><img alt="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587591372p2/33135672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1034800738?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " href="/user/show/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner">Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner?shelf=businessmen">businessmen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner?shelf=most-anticipated">most-anticipated</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1034800738" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17509419668736403378"><i>
  <b> 4.5 omfg stars </b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450641712i/17450796.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have to admit that I was debating between 4-5 stars, so this will take 4.5 stars from me. It certainly was a better installment to the first book, 'Debt Inheritance'. <br/><br/>I enjoyed the First Debt way more than the first one. I remember being frustrated after reading Debt Inheritance. I remember how much I <i> loathed </i> Jethro. I remember being even a fan of Kestrel and I was shipping him with Nila. <br/><br/>Well, guess what? <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398980935ra/9492902.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And boy, did the MCs in this book changed! Whoah! I couldn't belie</span>
  <span id="freeText17509419668736403378" style="display:none"><i>
  <b> 4.5 omfg stars </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450641712i/17450796.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to admit that I was debating between 4-5 stars, so this will take 4.5 stars from me. It certainly was a better installment to the first book, 'Debt Inheritance'. <br><br>I enjoyed the First Debt way more than the first one. I remember being frustrated after reading Debt Inheritance. I remember how much I <i> loathed </i> Jethro. I remember being even a fan of Kestrel and I was shipping him with Nila. <br><br>Well, guess what? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398980935ra/9492902.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And boy, did the MCs in this book changed! Whoah! I couldn't believe how much Jet had changed in this sequel. It was like reading an entirely different character. I was so shocked that at first it didn't sit well with me. Such a rapid change of character? Like I said, it was like it wasn't the same character &amp; I was a little disappointed to be honest. <br><br>BUT moving through the book I could see what was really going on. What was hidden beneath his character &amp; I have to admit that I enjoyed his character development. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450640211i/17450718.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But what I enjoyed most was Nila's character development. The weak fashion artist we knew from the first part with the constant vertigo issues? She's got some balls &amp; I certainly enjoyed how she changed throughout this sequel. I can't wait to see more of her in the next installment. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450640211i/17450719.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to say that I really admire Pepper's writing. She needs a damn applause for this. I loved the raging war between Jethro &amp; Nila. I loved how their constant meetings were always a battle of who would win and who would lose. Who was the hunter &amp; who was the prey. I enjoyed watching things becoming reversed. Nila going after Jethro &amp; him trying to pull away from her. I'm such a happy reader thanks to her. <br><br><b>
  <i> We couldn’t deny what’d just happened.<br>It wasn’t just sex. It wasn’t just lust.<br>It was something more. </i>
</b><br><br>What I can't say I enjoyed was that, even though I accidentally spoiled myself about Kite's identity, I have to say that it was the only thing predictable while reading this book. Yes, I already knew who he was while reading, but still, it seemed too obvious. <br><br>Nonetheless, I would encourage people to read this series. And I know that the first one may not be very pleasant, but keep reading, because this one definitely explains a lot &amp; it doesn't disappoint! :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416159202ra/11904412.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1060320609" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1060320609" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1060320609?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=dark-and-gritty">dark-and-gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=abused">abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-steam-alert">high-steam-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=rich-hottie">rich-hottie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=my-heart-can-barely-take-it">my-heart-can-barely-take-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1060320609" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15426988273814226659"> <b>"Empathy and softness weren’t permitted. They were the root of all evil for a person like me."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427517486i/14279395.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>First Debt is the second book in the Indebted series. All I can say is Pepper Winters has one fantastic imagination. From the first book we have learned that Nila has been taken captive by the Hawk family. She is now the property of Jethro Hawk. The first book was full of horrors as Nila is just trying to come to terms with the situation she has been forced into! Jethro gives her the chance to run but</span>
  <span id="freeText15426988273814226659" style="display:none"> <b>"Empathy and softness weren’t permitted. They were the root of all evil for a person like me."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427517486i/14279395.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>First Debt is the second book in the Indebted series. All I can say is Pepper Winters has one fantastic imagination. From the first book we have learned that Nila has been taken captive by the Hawk family. She is now the property of Jethro Hawk. The first book was full of horrors as Nila is just trying to come to terms with the situation she has been forced into! Jethro gives her the chance to run but if she is caught she must agree to his terms. <br><br>In the very beginning of First Debt Nila is running. You can't help but have hope that she will get away. But we know the truth- if she does get away the book will be over! The inevitable is she will get caught. The only question is: what will Jethro do to her when she does?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427517486i/14279396._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jethro doesn't know what to think of Nila. (The truth is we don't know what to think of Jethro either). This heroine evokes a plethora of emotions from this hero. Emotions that he has tried to keep blocked off.<br><br> <b>"How could I understand and keep my bearings when the bloody woman had more personalities than a Picasso painting? Sometimes naïve. Sometimes coy. Smart, fearful, proud, gullible. And above all, evolving."-Jethro </b><br><br>Nila is going through so much. She is certainly living through PTSD after everything she has already been through. Not to mention the anxiety of not knowing what is to come.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427517486i/14279397.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Truthfully she is finding herself. Somewhere through the torture and despair she is becoming stronger.<br><br> <b>"The collar on my throat was heavy, but at least it had warmed. The diamonds no longer felt alien but a part of me. The courage of my ancestors. The spirit-strength of women I’d never met, living in a piece of jewelry throbbing with their guidance and energy."-Nila</b><br><br>The one thing Nila is certain of. She feels something for Jethro. She knows that if she can get him to kiss her she can gain some control back over this crazy situation.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427517486i/14279398._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Jethro finally concedes and gives into his desires, it is game over. The floodgates open and Jethro looses all control over his drive to have her. The connection between the two is definitely high on octane. One thing Jethro knows, she is his and he is not going to share. <br><br> <b>"Now, I would never be able to share. Never. She was mine."-Jethro</b><br><br> The physical connection between the two is undeniable.<br><br> <b>"He was perfect. Utterly perfect. Our foreheads crashed together as he sank deeper and deeper."-NIla</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427518361i/14279469._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is the emotions that are still in question. Does Nila feel love for him? Is Jethro even capable of loving someone? <br><br>My heart hurts for Jethro. It is painfully clear that Nila is a means to an end. He feels trapped. His family has a hold on him and if he ever wants to break free Nila is the key. <br><br> <b>"Hate and love… they were the same thing. I’d tried to harness only one— hate. I tried to be my father’s son, full of mistrust for others, while asserting dominance and fear."-Jethro</b><br><br>Nila continues to form a friendship with Jethro's brother. She thinks that she knows him. The truth is Nila doesn't know anything.<br><br> <b>"It wasn’t ideal. It probably wasn’t healthy. But it was the best damn relationship I’d ever had."-Nila</b><br><br>Overall, First Debt only increased my anxiety over Nila's fate. Will she ever recover from this or will she have to check into a mental institution? While reading this, I longed for more emotional connection for Jethro and Nila. I hope that as their relationship continues to develop it will come. The dual POV keeps Jethro human. It is critical to see that Nila isn't the only one struggling. The intensity in the story is continually driving forward. The need to understand what cannot be understood outweighs any questions of logic. In other words, when reading this book just buckle up because it is going to be a bumpy ride. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427518884i/14279546._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15426988273814226659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1028478049" />
    <a title="✿kawehi.reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12789361-kawehi-reviews"><img alt="✿kawehi.reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425331136p2/12789361.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1028478049?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✿kawehi.reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✿kawehi.reviews" href="/user/show/12789361-kawehi-reviews">✿kawehi.reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12789361-kawehi-reviews?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1028478049" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10041809343226771193">☆ I received an ARC via TSOR PR in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!! ☆<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415672914i/11827776._SX540_.jpg' alt='pizap com14156721406011' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>What in the world goes on in the mind of Pepper Winters? This lady seriously is crafty in upping the stakes in this sensual yet gritty, twisted, and controversial trilogy!</i>
</b><br/><br/>I swear, at the ending of book one, I was hyperventilating for Nila when Jethro presented the opportunity for her to get away. The questions it left in its wake were- will Nila do it? Is Jethro for real or just messing/or toying with her? And wha</span>
  <span id="freeText10041809343226771193" style="display:none">☆ I received an ARC via TSOR PR in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!! ☆<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415672914i/11827776._SX540_.jpg" alt="pizap com14156721406011" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>What in the world goes on in the mind of Pepper Winters? This lady seriously is crafty in upping the stakes in this sensual yet gritty, twisted, and controversial trilogy!</i>
</b><br><br>I swear, at the ending of book one, I was hyperventilating for Nila when Jethro presented the opportunity for her to get away. The questions it left in its wake were- will Nila do it? Is Jethro for real or just messing/or toying with her? And what is the catch?<br><br><b>
  <i>First Debt</i>
</b> really intensifies the fight for survival and Nila’s will to never back down. Sure, she’s in a sh*&amp;y predicament, but I loved how her character grew and toughened throught her ordeal.<br><br>As for Jethro, well, I LOVED <i>yet</i> <s>HATED</s> him so much at first and throughout the first part of this installment but there was some inkling of light that there is some sort of vulnerable, humanity to him.<br><br>I’m DEFINITELY 100% on board for book 3 to see what further antes will be on he line and what will happen forward on! Gah!! The probabilities the author presents!!<br><br>I need MORE!!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1033365711" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1033365711" />
    <a title="Kirsten" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23049700-kirsten"><img alt="Kirsten" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426126650p2/23049700.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1033365711?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsten" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsten" href="/user/show/23049700-kirsten">Kirsten</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23557078-first-debt">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23049700-kirsten?shelf=edge-of-my-seat">edge-of-my-seat</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23049700-kirsten?shelf=guys-who-capture">guys-who-capture</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23049700-kirsten?shelf=total-mind-fuck">total-mind-fuck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23049700-kirsten?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23049700-kirsten?shelf=so-freaking-hot">so-freaking-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23049700-kirsten?shelf=it-s-dark-in-here">it-s-dark-in-here</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1033365711" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11760104829820360118"><b> 4.5 I heart Jethro stars! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg1_zps86eda940.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934904.jpg' alt=' photo imagejpg1_zps86eda940.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Whew! <br/>Mind, is blown. Heart, is still beating fast. Head, is confused. Body, is still on fire. That was intense! <br/><br/>At the end of book 1, we were left in anticipation of Nila running for her freedom. The poor girl is starved, tired, naked, and suffers from vertigo. Not to mention the horrendous luncheon she had just attended. Her head and body are in the worst predicament to run for her life. Yet still she tries. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg2_zps6aefc44d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934905.jpg' alt=' photo imagejpg2_zps6aefc44d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>From here on out, there is a battle of wits between</span>
  <span id="freeText11760104829820360118" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 I heart Jethro stars! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg1_zps86eda940.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934904.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps86eda940.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Whew! <br>Mind, is blown. Heart, is still beating fast. Head, is confused. Body, is still on fire. That was intense! <br><br>At the end of book 1, we were left in anticipation of Nila running for her freedom. The poor girl is starved, tired, naked, and suffers from vertigo. Not to mention the horrendous luncheon she had just attended. Her head and body are in the worst predicament to run for her life. Yet still she tries. <br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg2_zps6aefc44d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934905.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg2_zps6aefc44d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>From here on out, there is a battle of wits between the two. Nila is accepting of her fate, but she is going to do her damnedest to try to flip the switches on the Hawks, and stop the debt once and for all. <br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg5_zps282f9cec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934906.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg5_zps282f9cec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Both characters are battling with an onslaught of different emotions. Nila wants her revenge and is going to do all she can to stay strong. Jethro is dealing with new feelings. His icy layer is starting to thaw. The two can't help the lust/ hate relationship that they have. Who will come out on top, when it comes to the mind games they are playing? <br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg7_zpsd2897af3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934907.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg7_zpsd2897af3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Revelations are made when the "first debt" is paid (we still have no clue how many debts there are). Nila finds out more about her family's history. And Jethro is becoming more enamored with his property. <br><br> <a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg4_zps96a5e2fe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934908.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg4_zps96a5e2fe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nila is also sure she has the evidence she needs to know who the mysterious Kite007 is. She is going to use this knowledge in hopes of gaining trust and having an ally. Even with the sexting going on, Nila's body has a magnetic pull toward the cold Jethro. Dueling her need to hopefully get Jethro to open up, and to satisfy her own desires, she wants one thing. A simple kiss. But he is not as willing to give her what she wants. <br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg3_zpse32da730.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934909.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg3_zpse32da730.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Through all this mind fuckery, the underlying sexual tension is at an all time high. However, the consequences could be even higher. <br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg6_zps3ad72d4b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416319256i/11934910._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg6_zps3ad72d4b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This was an awesome sequel to the first book. We got some answers, and even more questions. <br><br>I am loving this series. It encompasses all of the elements in a great read for me. The story is original and paced very well. It has plenty of dark elements, and strong characters. The suspense and the "brain screw" is keeping me on the edge of my seat. And the sexual tension....holy shit, it's through the roof. When they finally give in, it's really intense and angry. So fucking hot! :P<br><br>So why not 5 stars from me? <br>Well as much as I loved everything, the thoughts of the MC's started to get to be <b>too</b> much. I definitely understand that the circumstances involved with both of them are extreme and are causing a lot of mixed feelings, but their mental duality was starting to make my head spin and get frustrating. I liked that they had conflicting emotions, but I think it was reiterated more than necessary. <br><br>The ending was shocking, and I am excited for the next book to come out. I have so many questions.... I can't wait to see what unfolds for Nila and Jethro. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11760104829820360118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HdOz3zFO9kJfr12ztqV7on6+tDL0GT83L5Jq/qFqYi9/eel2e1pqne0rkkjjADpA6zaeq+pkP60dDIpwBni1kw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wob0UhqxzY2DB2kQKCqXXpnm4v5Rmu6XSExEb31uXdCgLK77UKVRUjGDput9j9a8DG7IZ0/n7g160qTh2nyKbA==')})
  }
